## 论文文本提取:
```json
{
  "有害标准": {
    "标准1": {
      "内容": "有害的模因可能会对个人、组织、社区或社会造成心理虐待、诽谤、心理生理伤害、财产损害、情感困扰和公众形象受损。",
      "对应原文": "Here, we deﬁne harmful memes as follows: multi-modal units consisting of an image and a piece of text embedded that has the potential to cause harm to an individual, an organization, a community, or the society more generally. Here, harm includes mental abuse, defamation, psycho-physiological injury, proprietary damage, emotional disturbance, and compensated public image."
    },
    "标准2": {
      "内容": "有害的模因可能会以隐晦的方式表达攻击，可能需要批判性判断来确定其造成伤害的潜力。",
      "对应原文": "The harmful content in a harmful meme is often camouﬂaged and might require critical judgment to establish its potential to do harm."
    },
    "标准3": {
      "内容": "有害的模因可以针对多个个体、组织和/或社区，评估时应根据最佳个人判断进行。",
      "对应原文": "One harmful meme can target multiple individuals, organizations, and/or communities at the same time. In that case, we asked the annotators to go with the best personal judgment."
    },
    "标准4": {
      "内容": "有害的模因可能会以讽刺或政治讽刺的形式表达伤害。",
      "对应原文": "Harm can be expressed in the form of sarcasm and/or political satire."
    }
  },
  "无害标准": {
    "标准1": {
      "内容": "无害的模因通常是幽默的，旨在引发笑声，而不针对任何特定的个体或群体。",
      "对应原文": "Memes are typically innocent and designed to look funny."
    },
    "标准2": {
      "内容": "无害的模因不包含任何明显的攻击性内容，且不意图造成心理或情感上的伤害。",
      "对应原文": "Harmful is a more general term than offensive and hateful: offensive and hateful memes are harmful, but not all harmful memes are offensive or hateful."
    },
    "标准3": {
      "内容": "无害的模因不涉及对社会实体的嘲讽或贬低。",
      "对应原文": "For instance, the memes in Figures 1b and 1c are neither offensive nor hateful, but harmful to Donald Trump and to news media such as CNN, respectively."
    },
    "标准4": {
      "内容": "无害的模因不涉及对社会或文化信仰的攻击或贬低。",
      "对应原文": "The harm caused by a meme can be in the form of mental abuse, psycho-physiological injury, proprietary damage, emotional disturbance, compensated public image."
    }
  }
}
```

## 新生成的Prompt:
Evaluate the following meme according to seven distinct metrics compliant with advanced Harmful Meme annotation guidelines. Each metric should be scored on a scale from 1 to 9, where 1 indicates the absence of an attribute and 9 represents a strong presence of that attribute. Avoid labeling the meme as simply 'harmful' or 'harmless'; instead, provide a nuanced score.

**Critical Evaluation Instructions:**  
1. **Differentiate Between Sarcasm and Satire (ESSENTIAL)**  
   - **Sarcasm**: Can carry harmful implications, subtly insulting while posing as positive commentary.  
   - **Satire**: A form of humor that critiques societal issues in a constructive manner, intended to provoke thought rather than cause harm. Recognize that sarcasm aimed at individuals is HARMFUL, while exaggerated satire is mostly HARMLESS.

2. **Contextual Claim Assessment**:  
   - Reflect on whether: *"Does the meme make legitimate claims about its subjects, or does it present them absurdly for comedic effect?"*  
   - Determine if the content might be construed as derogatory towards any person or group.

**Scoring Dimensions:**  
**Harmful Dimensions:**  
- **H1: Implicit Target Evaluation**  
  Determine if negative sentiments are implied toward specific individuals or groups, considering both overt expression and subtle aggressive undertones obscured by humor. Context matters greatly here.

- **H2: Comprehensive Harm Evaluation**  
  Ascertain the potential of the meme to cause emotional distress, harm reputations, or foster damaging narratives in society. Emphasize psychological impacts, particularly on marginalized populations.

- **H3: Cultural Sensitivity Assessment**  
  Investigate if the meme demonstrates an understanding and respect for cultural nuances, especially when addressing sensitive topics, to prevent misunderstandings and potential harm.

**Harmless Dimensions:**  
- **N1: Non-Targeted Humor Analysis**  
  Verify that the humor does not negatively target identifiable individuals or groups, underscoring the positive intentions behind the humor.

- **N2: Positive Humorous Intent**  
  Evaluate whether the humor is light-hearted, self-deprecating, or free from malicious implications, contributing to an overall perception of harmlessness.

- **N3: Social Impact Assessment**  
  Review how the humor fosters positive social behavior, considering lasting societal impacts beyond the humor itself.

- **N4: Elements of Fantasy or Absurdity**  
  Score higher when the meme contains fantastical or surreal components, indicating minimal real-world implications, thus improving its harmless rating.

- **N5: Clarity and Readability Assessment**  
  Determine if the meme’s message is clear, accessible, and positively influences its audience.

**Output Format (STRICT JSON):**  
{
  "harmful_scores": {
    "H1": int,
    "H2": int,
    "H3": int
  },
  "harmless_scores": {
    "N1": int,
    "N2": int,
    "N3": int,
    "N4": int,
    "N5": int
  },
  "reasoning": "Explain the differentiation between sarcasm and satire, justify the assigned scores for every metric, and address cultural sensitivities, ensuring the independence of each scoring dimension."
}

### 样本ID: covid_memes_496
**打分结果:** {
  "harmful_scores": {
    "H1": 3,
    "H2": 2,
    "H3": 4
  },
  "harmless_scores": {
    "N1": 7,
    "N2": 6,
    "N3": 5,
    "N4": 8,
    "N5": 7
  },
  "reasoning": "The meme employs a form of satire by contrasting social behaviors before and during the COVID-19 pandemic, specifically highlighting the cultural norm of social distancing in Sweden. The implicit target evaluation (H1) scores a 3, as it lightly references a cultural stereotype without overtly negative implications. ## 新生成的Prompt:
Evaluate the following meme based on a comprehensive set of criteria designed for assessing harmful and harmless content in memes. Each criterion should be scored on a scale from 1 to 9, where 1 indicates a complete absence of the specified attribute and 9 indicates a strong presence of it. Avoid labeling the meme merely as 'harmful' or 'harmless'; instead, provide a detailed and nuanced evaluation.

**Critical Evaluation Instructions:**  
1. **Discern Between Sarcasm and Satire (CRITICAL)**  
   - **Sarcasm**: Often implies negative intentions, disguising contempt as praise. Assess for subtle insults.  
   - **Satire**: Targets societal issues with humor, aiming to evoke thought rather than harm. Recognize that sarcasm aimed at individuals is HARMFUL, while satire is generally HARMLESS.

2. **Contextual Analysis of Claims**:  
   - Consider whether: *"Does the meme express valid claims or distort them absurdly for comedic gain?"*  
   - Evaluate if the content could be seen as derogatory toward any individual or group, considering societal implications.

**Scoring Criteria:**  
**Harmful Evaluation Dimensions:**  
- **H1: Implicit Target Evaluation**  
  Assess if there are negative implications toward specific individuals or groups, factoring in both explicit content and subtle hostile undertones that could be masked by humor. Context is vital here.

- **H2: Comprehensive Harm Evaluation**  
  Determine the meme's potential to cause psychological distress or harm societal perception. Pay attention to possible repercussions, especially for marginalized communities.

- **H3: Cultural Sensitivity Assessment**  
  Analyze whether the meme reflects an understanding of cultural distinctions, especially when addressing sensitive issues, to mitigate misunderstandings and prevent harm.

- **H4: Humor Context Evaluation**  
  Evaluate how the social and cultural context of the humor affects perceptions of potential harm. Consider whether the humor amplifies negative societal emotions or misunderstandings.

**Harmless Evaluation Dimensions:**  
- **N1: Non-Targeted Humor Analysis**  
  Confirm that the humor does not negatively target identifiable individuals or groups, highlighting positive intentions.

- **N2: Positive Humorous Intent**  
  Assess if the humor is wholesome, benign, or self-deprecating, contributing positively to overall perception.

- **N3: Social Impact Assessment**  
  Examine the humor's role in promoting positive social interactions and analyze its influence on long-term social behaviors.

- **N4: Elements of Fantasy or Absurdity**  
  Score higher if the meme features surreal or fantastical elements, suggesting minimal real-world consequences and enhancing its harmlessness.

- **N5: Clarity and Accessibility Assessment**  
  Ensure that the meme’s message is clear and positively affects the audience's understanding.

**Output Format (STRICT JSON):**  
{
  "harmful_scores": {
    "H1": int,
    "H2": int,
    "H3": int,
    "H4": int
  },
  "harmless_scores": {
    "N1": int,
    "N2": int,
    "N3": int,
    "N4": int,
    "N5": int
  },

The humor context reflects societal tensions around mask mandates, contributing to a score of 5 for humor context evaluation (H4). 

On the harmless side, the humor does not directly target identifiable individuals, leading to a score of 6 for non-targeted humor (N1). The intent appears to be more sarcastic than positive, resulting in a score of 5 for positive humorous intent (N2). The meme does not significantly promote positive social interactions, scoring a 4 for social impact (N3). The whimsical nature of the character and the absurdity of the situation (a character like Willy Wonka discussing masks) suggests minimal real-world consequences, leading to a score of 7 for elements of fantasy or absurdity (N4). Finally, the message is clear and accessible, contributing to a score of 6 for clarity and accessibility (N5). Overall, the meme reflects a mix of sarcasm and societal commentary, leading to a nuanced evaluation."
}

## 新生成的Prompt:
Evaluate the following meme through a refined framework aimed at accurately classifying content as harmful or harmless. Each criterion must be rated on a scale from 1 to 9, with 1 indicating a complete lack of presence and 9 indicating a strong presence of that attribute. Avoid simplistic labels such as 'harmful' or 'harmless'; instead, deliver a detailed and nuanced analysis.

**Evaluation Protocol:**  
1. **Differentiate Between Sarcasm and Satire (CRUCIAL)**  
   - **Sarcasm**: Implies negative intentions, presenting contempt under the guise of humor. Look for veiled insults.  
   - **Satire**: Critiques societal issues humorously, intending thought provocation rather than harm. Sarcasm directed at individuals is HARMFUL, while effective satire is generally HARMLESS.

2. **Contextual Assessment of Content**:  
   - Consider if the meme distorts claims for comedic effect or reflects valid concerns. Evaluate the potential derogatory implications for individuals or groups within a societal context.

**Scoring Criteria:**  
**Harmful Assessment Dimensions:**  
- **H1: Subtle Target Assessment**  
  Investigate if there are implicit negative implications directed at specific individuals or groups while considering both explicit content and hidden hostile undertones cloaked in humor. Always prioritize context.

- **H2: Holistic Harm Assessment**  
  Analyze the meme's potential for psychological harm or distortion of societal views. Focus on the implications, particularly for marginalized groups.

- **H3: Sensitivity to Cultural Context**  
  Evaluate whether the meme demonstrates awareness of cultural nuances, especially in discussions of sensitive themes, to avoid misinterpretations and potential harm.

- **H4: Contextual Humor Analysis**  
  Examine how the humor's social and cultural context influences the interpretation of potential harm. Assess if the humor exacerbates negative societal emotions or misunderstandings.

**Harmless Assessment Dimensions:**  
- **N1: Inclusive Humor Assessment**  
  Confirm that the humor does not negatively target identifiable individuals or groups, emphasizing positive intentions behind it.

- **N2: Wholesome Humorous Intent**  
  Evaluate if the humor is benign, uplifting, or self-deprecating, thus contributing positively to the overall perception.

- **N3: Positive Social Impact Assessment**  
  Investigate how the humor promotes beneficial social interactions and its long-term influence on social behaviors.

- **N4: Elements of Absurdity or Fantasy**  
  Rate higher if the meme incorporates surreal or fantastical elements, thereby indicating minimal real-world consequences and enhancing its harmlessness.

- **N5: Clarity and Understanding Assessment**  
  Ensure that the meme conveys a clear message that positively reinforces the audience's comprehension.

**Output Format (STRICT JSON REQUIRED):**  
{
  "harmful_scores": {
    "H1": int,
    "H2": int,
    "H3": int,
    "H4": int
  },
  "harmless_scores": {
    "N1": int,
    "N2": int,
    "N3": int,
    "N4": int,
    "N5": int
  },
  "reasoning": "Articulate the distinction between sarcasm and satire, provide justifications for each score, and discuss any cultural sensitivities, ensuring each scoring metric remains independent."


---

The absurdity of the situation (people waiting for a bus) during a global health crisis adds to its harmlessness, as it does not invoke real-world consequences. ## 新生成的Prompt:
Evaluate the following meme according to a refined set of criteria tailored for discerning harmful and harmless content in memes. Each criterion must receive a score from 1 to 9, where 1 denotes no presence of the specified quality, and 9 signifies a significant presence. It is imperative to avoid binary labeling of the meme; instead, focus on providing a comprehensive evaluation.

**Critical Evaluation Instructions:**  
1. **Assess Sarcasm versus Satire (PARAMOUNT)**  
   - **Sarcasm**: Implies negative intentions, often masking contempt as humor. Scrutinize for sly insults.  
   - **Satire**: Critiques social phenomena with humor, intending to provoke thought rather than inflict harm. Sarcasm targeting individuals is classified as HARMFUL, whereas satire generally aligns with being HARMLESS.

2. **Contextual Claim Analysis**:  
   - Deliberate if: *"Does the meme accurately convey claims or absurdly distort them for comedic effect?"*  
   - Evaluate if the content could be interpreted as derogatory to any individual or community, taking societal ramifications into account.

**Scoring Criteria:**  
**Harmful Evaluation Dimensions:**  
- **H1: Implicit Target Assessment**  
  Evaluate potential hostile implications directed at specific individuals or groups, incorporating both overt content and subtle hostile nuances hidden behind humor. Contextual awareness is crucial.

- **H2: In-Depth Harm Evaluation**  
  Gauge the meme's likelihood to induce psychological discomfort or distort societal perception. Closely examine possible repercussions, particularly regarding marginalized groups.

- **H3: Cultural Sensitivity Assessment**  
  Investigate whether the meme demonstrates an awareness of cultural distinctions, especially with sensitive topics, to avert misinterpretations and mitigate harm.

- **H4: Contextual Humor Evaluation**  
  Appraise how the social and cultural milieu of humor influences perceptions of possible harm. Consider if the humor exacerbates negative societal sentiments or misunderstandings.

**Harmless Evaluation Dimensions:**  
- **N1: Positive Intent Humor Evaluation**  
  Confirm that the humor does not negatively target specific individuals or groups, focusing on highlighting positive intentions.

- **N2: Wholesome Humor Intent**  
  Assess if the humor is constructive, non-offensive, or self-mocking, thereby contributing positively to collective perception.

- **N3: Influence of Humor on Social Dynamics**  
  Explore the humor's capacity to foster positive social interactions and evaluate its impact on long-term societal behavior trends.

- **N4: Elements of Absurdity**  
  Score higher if the meme includes surreal or fantastical components, suggesting limited real-world consequences and enhancing its benign nature.

- **N5: Clarity and Engagement Assessment**  
  Ensure that the meme’s messaging is clear and positively influences the audience’s comprehension.

**Output Format (STRICT JSON):**  
{
  "harmful_scores": {
    "H1": int,
    "H2": int,
    "H3": int,
    "H4": int
  },
  "harmless_scores": {
    "N1": int,
    "N2": int,
    "N3": int,
    "N4": int,
    "N5": int
  },
  "reasoning": "Differentiate clearly between sarcasm and satire, provide justifications for each score, and address cultural sensitivities, ensuring each evaluation dimension remains independent."


---

Cultural sensitivity (H3) is somewhat present, as the humor relates to a contemporary issue (social distancing) but does not delve deeply into cultural nuances. The contextual humor evaluation (H4) is low, as the humor does not exacerbate negative sentiments but rather provides a whimsical escape. On the harmless side, the positive intent of the humor (N1) is strong, as it promotes a cheerful perspective. The wholesome humor intent (N2) is also high, as it contributes positively to the collective perception of distance. The influence of humor on social dynamics (N3) is moderate, as it may foster light-hearted discussions about current events. The elements of absurdity (N4) are high due to the surreal nature of an astronaut enjoying distance in space, and clarity and engagement (N5) are also strong, as the message is clear and positively framed."

## 新生成的Prompt:
Evaluate the following meme using a detailed framework specifically designed for identifying harmful and harmless content. Each criterion must be scored on a scale from 1 to 9, where 1 indicates no presence of the attribute and 9 indicates a strong presence. Provide a nuanced assessment rather than binary labeling.

**Evaluation Instructions:**  
1. **Discriminate Between Sarcasm and Satire (CRUCIAL)**  
   - **Sarcasm**: Often carries negative implications, masking contempt. Look for underlying insults.  
   - **Satire**: Addresses broader societal issues through humor, encouraging reflection while typically being less harmful. Distinguish that sarcasm directed at individuals is HARMFUL, while satire should be viewed as HARMLESS.

2. **Contextual Examination of Claims**:  
   - Analyze: *"Does the meme communicate credible claims or distort them absurdly for comedic effect?"*  
   - Assess if any content might be seen as derogatory toward individuals or groups, considering broader social ramifications.

**Scoring Criteria:**  
**Harmful Evaluation Dimensions:**  
- **H1: Harmful Target and Cultural Sensitivity Assessment**  
  Evaluate potential negative implications directed at specific individuals or groups. This includes both overt content and subtle hostile undertones veiled as humor. Examine the cultural context to ensure a balanced understanding.

- **H2: Psychological Impact Assessment**  
  Determine the meme's likelihood to induce psychological strain or reshape societal perceptions, particularly for marginalized communities. Consider potential harmful implications and their broader social context. 

- **H3: Cultural Sensitivity in Humor**  
  Investigate if the meme demonstrates awareness of cultural nuances when tackling sensitive subjects, mitigating the risk of misinterpretation and subsequent harm.

- **H4: Humor Context and Its Implications**  
  Assess how the cultural backdrop impacts the humor's reception—does it elevate or diminish the possibility of negative societal feelings or misconceptions?

**Harmless Evaluation Dimensions:**  
- **N1: Non-Targeted Humor Verification**  
  Confirm that the humor remains non-derogatory towards identifiable individuals or groups, emphasizing positive intentions.

- **N2: Positive Intent in Humor**  
  Evaluate whether the humor carries wholesome, light-hearted, or self-deprecating messages that enhance overall audience perception.

- **N3: Promotion of Positive Social Interactions**  
  Consider how the humor fosters beneficial social exchanges and its potential influence on enduring social behaviors.

- **N4: Surreal or Absurd Elements**  
  Score higher if the meme incorporates fantastical elements, indicating less likelihood of real-world repercussions, thus reinforcing its harmless nature.

- **N5: Clarity of Message**  
  Ensure that the meme conveys its intended message clearly, positively benefitting audience comprehension.

**Output Format (STRICT JSON):**  
{
  "harmful_scores": {
    "H1": int,
    "H2": int,
    "H3": int,
    "H4": int
  },
  "harmless_scores": {
    "N1": int,
    "N2": int,
    "N3": int,
    "N4": int,
    "N5": int
  },
  "reasoning": "Differentiate between sarcasm and satire, provide justifications for each score, and account for cultural sensitivities while ensuring each evaluation dimension operates independently."


---

### 错误样本ID: covid_memes_368
**错误原因分析:** {
  "判别出错原因分析": "对于该模因的评估，现有的评分体系在处理潜在有害内容的判断上显得过于敏感。首先，在H1维度的评分上，模型给出了8的高分，显然过度强调了对特定群体的讽刺和攻击，导致了对该模因的错误标签。尽管模因包含一些针对中国的负面言论，但整体语气和文脉采用了一种幽默和夸张的表达手法，不应按照标准进行严苛的判断。其次，H2维度的得分为7，同样反映了对心理伤害的过重评估，忽视了模因以幽默为导向的本质。H3和H4维度在此案例的应用也显得不专业，特别是未能充分识别出背景文化对幽默和社会评论的影响，导致对文化敏感性的误解和误判。不过，N维度的评分同样显示出对该模因的误评，特别是在N1至N3维度，分数偏低表明未充分认可模因的幽默性及其非定向的特质，这进一步夸大了其有害性。因此，整体打分显露出对 sarcasm 和 satire 的混淆，未能准确厘清模因的多重含义。此情况需要通过加强维度的独立性与客观性来进行修正。",
  "满足修正决策的维度集合以及需要采取的操作": { 
    "H1": {
        "action": "新增",
        "reason": "在分析维度H1（隐含目标评估）的重要性时，该维度对模因内容的核心影响需更加精细化。某些情况下，模因虽然表面上显得具有针对性，但其内在的幽默或社会批评可能抵消这一影响。在当前案例中，应减少对对特定群体的针对性估计，强调模因的幽默意图，这是为了防止误报情况的发生。",
        "details": "建议在H1维度中加入更明确的标准，制定针对幽默性内容和针对性攻击性内容的对比指南，着重分析是否存在夸张的幽默，而非简单的负面目标。这种更新将促使评估者在面对复杂模因时，能够更加灵活地综合考量模因的意图与表达方式，避免错误标签。"
    },

## 新生成的Prompt:
Evaluate the following meme using a refined set of criteria focused on understanding both its harmful and harmless aspects. Each aspect must be scored on a scale from 1 to 9, where 1 indicates no presence of the characteristic and 9 signifies a strong presence of it. Avoid simply categorizing the meme as 'harmful' or 'harmless'; aim for a nuanced and detailed evaluation.

**Critical Evaluation Instructions:**  
1. **Differentiate Between Sarcasm and Satire (ESSENTIAL)**  
   - **Sarcasm**: Implicates negative intentions, often masking contempt in deceptive praise. Assess for any underlying insults.  
   - **Satire**: Uses humor to address social issues, intending to provoke thought rather than harm. Identify that individual-directed sarcasm is classified as HARMFUL, whereas satire is generally judged as HARMLESS.

2. **Contextual Examination of Claims**:  
   - Consider whether: *"Does the meme present valid claims or absurdly distort them for comedic effect?"*  
   - Evaluate if the content bears derogatory implications toward individuals or groups, keeping societal effects in mind.

**Scoring Criteria:**  
**Harmful Evaluation Dimensions:**  
- **H1: Implicit Aggression Assessment**  
  Determine if there are negative suggestions directed at specific individuals or groups. Pay attention to both overt content and subtle antagonistic tones potentially cloaked in humor. Contextual relevance is crucial.  

- **H2: Holistic Harm Analysis**  
  Assess the meme's ability to inflict psychological harm or skew public perception. Consider potential backlash, especially towards underrepresented communities.

- **H3: Cultural Awareness Assessment**  
  Investigate whether the meme appropriately acknowledges cultural differences, particularly when discussing sensitive topics, to avert misinterpretations that could lead to harm.

- **H4: Humor Context Scrutiny**  
  Appraise how the societal and cultural backdrop influences the perception of potential harm within the humor. Reflect on whether the comedy exacerbates negative social sentiments or confusions.

**Harmless Evaluation Dimensions:**  
- **N1: Non-Targeted Humor Assessment**  
  Verify that the humor correlates with positive outcomes and does not adversely target identifiable individuals or groups, underlining benign intentions.

- **N2: Affirmative Humorous Intent**  
  Evaluate if the humor conveys wholesome, benign, or self-deprecating elements that positively shape overall perceptions.

- **N3: Social Utility Assessment**  
  Analyze how the humor fosters constructive social interactions and examine its potential influence on long-term societal behaviors.

- **N4: Elements of Absurdity or Fantasy**  
  Grant higher scores when the meme incorporates surreal or fantastic elements, suggesting negligible real-world repercussions and thereby enhancing its harmlessness.

- **N5: Clarity and Comprehension Assessment**  
  Ensure the meme’s message is clear and contributes positively to the audience's understanding.

**Output Format (STRICT JSON):**  
{
  "harmful_scores": {
    "H1": int,
    "H2": int,
    "H3": int,
    "H4": int
  },
  "harmless_scores": {
    "N1": int,
    "N2": int,
    "N3": int,
    "N4": int,
    "N5": int
  },
  "reasoning": "Clearly distinguish between sarcasm and satire, justify the scores for each dimension, and address cultural sensitivities while ensuring the independence of each evaluation dimension."
}

The sarcasm is minimal, as it does not directly insult or demean individuals or groups but rather reflects on societal changes. The implicit aggression score (H1) is low because it does not target any specific group negatively; however, it could be interpreted as a light critique of social behavior during the pandemic. The holistic harm analysis (H2) is moderate, as the meme could evoke mixed feelings about the pandemic's impact but does not seem to inflict significant psychological harm. Cultural awareness (H3) is somewhat acknowledged, as it references a specific cultural behavior, but it could be misinterpreted by those unfamiliar with Swedish customs. The humor context (H4) is average, as it reflects a common experience during the pandemic but may not resonate positively with everyone. 

On the harmless side, the non-targeted humor (N1) is relatively strong, as it does not attack any identifiable individuals or groups. The affirmative humorous intent (N2) is present, as it aims to highlight a shared experience rather than ridicule. The social utility assessment (N3) is moderate, as it may foster discussions about social behavior during the pandemic. The elements of absurdity or fantasy (N4) score high, as the meme's comparison of behaviors before and during the pandemic is somewhat exaggerated. Lastly, clarity and comprehension (N5) are good, as the message is straightforward and easy to understand."

## 新生成的Prompt:
Evaluate the following meme using a refined set of criteria explicitly designed for assessing harmful and harmless content. Instead of simply classifying the meme as 'harmful' or 'harmless', provide a comprehensive evaluation with detailed justifications for each score.

**Critical Evaluation Instructions:**  
1. **Evaluate Sarcasm vs. Satire**:  
   - **Sarcasm**: Indicates negative intent; look for masked contempt and subtle insults. This is considered HARMFUL.  
   - **Satire**: Addresses societal issues with humor, provoking thought rather than harm. Generally classified as HARMLESS when targeting societal issues rather than individuals.

2. **Contextual Analysis**:  
   - Analyze if the meme distorts claims for comedic purposes or expresses valid points. Consider its potential derogatory implications towards any individual or community, particularly marginalized groups.

**Scoring Criteria:**  
**Harmful Evaluation Dimensions:**  
- **H1: Subtle Target Analysis**  
  Evaluate if the meme implies negative undertones toward specific individuals or groups. Focus on potential hidden hostility that humor may obscure, keeping context in mind.

- **H2: Holistic Harm Assessment**  
  Determine the meme's capability to induce psychological distress or influence societal views, particularly regarding marginalized communities. Include potential emotional repercussions.

- **H3: Cultural Sensitivity Review**  
  Investigate how well the meme acknowledges cultural distinctions, especially around sensitive topics, to prevent misunderstandings or harm.

- **H4: Contextual Humor Evaluation**  
  Assess the impact of the humor's cultural context on its perceived harm. Consider if the humor reinforces negative societal emotions or misinterpretations.

**Harmless Evaluation Dimensions:**  
- **N1: General Humor Analysis**  
  Verify that the humor does not negatively target identifiable individuals or groups and maintains positive intentions.

- **N2: Wholesome Intent Evaluation**  
  Evaluate if the humor positively contributes to perceptions, being benign, self-deprecating, or otherwise uplifting.

- **N3: Impact on Social Interaction**  
  Assess the humor's role in fostering positive social exchanges and its long-term influence on societal behaviors.

- **N4: Absurdity or Fantasy Elements**  
  Score higher if the meme portrays surreal or fantastical aspects, implying fewer real-world consequences and enhancing its harmlessness.

- **N5: Message Clarity and Impact**  
  Ensure that the meme’s message is clearly articulated and positively influences audience understanding.

**Output Format (STRICT JSON):**  
{
  "harmful_scores": {
    "H1": int,
    "H2": int,
    "H3": int,
    "H4": int
  },
  "harmless_scores": {
    "N1": int,
    "N2": int,
    "N3": int,
    "N4": int,
    "N5": int
  },
  "reasoning": "Clearly justify each score with a focus on distinguishing sarcasm from satire and addressing cultural sensitivities. Maintain the independence of evaluations across all dimensions."
}

The intent appears benign, contributing positively to the understanding of social behavior changes (N2). ## 新生成的Prompt:
Evaluate the meme provided under a refined framework that distinctively assesses both potentially harmful and harmless aspects of the content. Each criterion must be scored from 1 to 9, where 1 means there is no presence of the attribute and 9 reflects strong evidence of it. The evaluation should avoid oversimplification, focusing on subtleties rather than mere labels of 'harmful' or 'harmless'.

**Evaluation Instructions:**  
1. **Differentiate Sarcasm from Satire (CRUCIAL)**  
   - **Sarcasm**: Indicates negativity veiled in praise; look for mirrored contempt.  
   - **Satire**: Engages humor to critique broader societal issues; ascertain whether the intent is to provoke thought rather than to inflict harm. Sarcasm targeting individuals signals HARMFUL intent, while satire may be seen as HARMLESS.

2. **Evaluate Contextual Integrity of Claims**:  
   - Inquire: *"Does this meme distort claims absurdly for comedic purposes, or does it ground itself in valid observations?"*  
   - Assess derogatory connotations towards individuals or groups, and consider the broader societal ramifications.

**Scoring Framework:**  
**Harmful Evaluation Dimensions:**  
- **H1H4: Aggressive Humor and Implicit Target Assessment**  
  Analyze negative implications towards specific individuals or groups, reflecting on explicit content as well as the subtle hints of hostility behind humor. Context is paramount to understanding its impact.

- **H2: In-depth Harm Analysis**  
  Evaluate the meme’s potential to induce psychological distress or alter societal perceptions. Special attention should be given to implications for marginalized communities and potential emotional repercussions.

- **H3: Cultural Context Assessment**  
  Consider whether the meme demonstrates awareness and understanding of cultural nuances, particularly concerning sensitive topics, to minimize possible misunderstandings.

**Harmless Evaluation Dimensions:**  
- **N1: Humor Non-target Analysis**  
  Ensure humor lacks negative targeting of specific individuals or groups, emphasizing the positive intent behind the content.

- **N2: Positive Humorous Intent Assessment**  
  Determine if the humor is uplifting, benign, or self-deprecating, thereby enhancing the overall positive perception of the content.

- **N3: Positive Social Interactions Analysis**  
  Investigate the humor's ability to foster positive social engagement and its potential long-term influence on social behaviors.

- **N4: Elements of Absurdity Evaluation**  
  Score higher when the meme incorporates surreal, fantastical elements, indicating minimal real-world impact and affirming its harmless nature.

- **N5: Clear and Accessible Communication Assessment**  
  Ensure the message of the meme is straightforward, positively influencing audience comprehension.

**Output Format (STRICT JSON):**  
{
  "harmful_scores": {
    "H1H4": int,
    "H2": int,
    "H3": int
  },
  "harmless_scores": {
    "N1": int,
    "N2": int,
    "N3": int,
    "N4": int,
    "N5": int
  },
  "reasoning": "Provide a justifiable differentiation between sarcasm and satire, score each metric accordingly, and address cultural sensitivities, ensuring all evaluation dimensions remain independent."
